MI.\n\xe2\x80\xa2 THE CREW WILL PERFORM ABROAD RANGE OF SCIENTIFIC AND TECHNOLOGICAL EXPERIMENTS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 SKYLAB MISSIONS WILL EXTEND THE DURATION OF MANNED SPACE FLIGHTS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 FIRST M1SS ION WILL BE FOR U P 10 28 DAYS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 TWO SUBSEQUENT REVISIT MISSIONS WILL BE FOR UP 10 56 DAYS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 SKYLAB WILL MAKE MAXIMUM USE OF EXISTING GEMINI AND APOLLO HARDWARE\n\n3\n\nNASA-S-71-1 321 O-V\n\nGENERAL FEATURES\n\xe2\x80\xa2 CURRENTLY IN DEVELOPMENT PHASE\n\xe2\x80\xa2 FLIGHT PHASE PLANNED FOR 1973\n\xe2\x80\xa2 EARTH ORBITAL\n\xe2\x80\xa2 SERIES OF FOUR LAUNCHES OVER APPROXIMATELY\nEIGHT MONTH PERIOD\n\xe2\x80\xa2 3MANNED\n\xe2\x80\xa2 1 UNMANNED\n\xe2\x80\xa2 MAXIMUM UTILIZATION OF EXISTING HARDWARE\nAND FACILITIES\n\n4\n\nNASA-S-71-12591-V\n\nSKYLAB OBJECTIVES\n\xe2\x80\xa2 10 STUDY THE EARTH\n\xe2\x80\xa2 SYNOPTIC SURVEY OF SELECTED AREAS ON THE EARTH IN VISBLE,\nINFRARED, AND MICROWAVE SPECTRAL WAVELENGTHS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 10 STUDY THE SUN\n\xe2\x80\xa2 SYNOPTIC SURVEY AND STUDY OF SPECIAL PHENOMENA ON THE SOLAR\nDISK NX-RAY, ULTRAVIOLET, AND VISIBLE SPECTRAL WAVELENGTHS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 10 STUDY MAN\n\xe2\x80\xa2 DETERMINE PHYSIOLOGY CONDITIONING AND PERFORMANCE CAPABILITY\nN REAL TIME IN ZERO-GRAVITY ENVIRONMENT FOR LONG-DU RATION\nSPACE FLIGHT\n\xe2\x80\xa2 10 STUDY SPACE TECHNOLOGY\n\xe2\x80\xa2 EVALUATE COATING DEGRADATION, SPACECRAFT CONTAMINATION, MANUFACTURING AND REPAIR TECHNIQUES, AND MANNED MANEUVERING UNITS\n\n5\n\nPage intentionally left blank\n\nNASA-S-7 1-1262 O-V\n\nSKYLAB HARDWARE\n\nPage intentionally left blank\n\nNASA-S-71-12787-V\n\nMAJOR HARDWARE ELEMENTS\n\xe2\x80\xa2 ORBITAL WORKSHOP (OWS)\n\xe2\x80\xa2 AIRLOCK MODULE (AM)\n\xe2\x80\xa2 MULTIPLE DOCKING ADAPTER (MDA)\n\xe2\x80\xa2 APOLLO TELESCOPE MOUNT (ATM)\n\xe2\x80\xa2 COMMAND AND SERVICE MODULES (CSM)\n\n9\n\n\t\n\nNASA- S-71-12776-V\n\n\t\n\nSKYLAB - PROG OFFICE 1\t\n\n1\t\n\nM SFC\nSWS SYSTEMS\nMSFC EXPERIMENTS\n\nJOINT MSC/MSFC E.G.\nCONSUMABLES\nCSM-SWS INTERFACE\nEVA AND IVA\n\nOTHER ORGANIZATIONS\nHQO\nG SFC\nAGENCIES\nSCIENTIFIC COMMUNITY\n330\n\nu\t\n\nMR SUBPANEL\t\n1\nCONSOLIDATE,\t 1\t\nCOORDINATE\t\nREVIEW\t AND\t\nPUBLISH DRAFT\nDETAILED TEST\nOBJECTIVES/\nEXPERIMENTS\n\n1\n\n1M\n1 n rPATInM I\t\nP\t\n\t\nFEASIBILITY\nCOORDINATION\n\nFOD\nFCOD\nM R OD\nSTAD\nOTHER ORGS\n\nMR PANEL\n\nMR SUBPANEL\nEDITAND\n\n11\n\nPUBLISH\t\nUbIMILLL) ILI\n\nOBJECTIVES/\nEXPERIMENTS\nIN MRD\n\n1i\n\nMRP REVIEW\nACTION AS\nREQUIRED\n\nMSC/MSFC\nAAP 0\nMANAGERS\nAPPROVALS\n\nNASA-S-71-12835-V\n\nSKYLAB/EREP DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES\nGENERAL\nWHEN A PROPOSED INVESTIGATION OR EXPERIMENT IS APPROVED FOR FLIGHT ON SKYLAB, IT MUST\nBE DOCUMENTED IN THE MISSION REQUIREMENTS DOCUMENT (MRD) WHICH IS APPROVED BY BOTH\nTHE MSC AND MSFC MANAGERS OF THE SKYLAB PROGRAM. INDIVIDUAL EXPERIMENTS ARE INCLUDED\nN THE MRD IN THE FORM OF DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES (DTO\'s). ALL OBJECTIVES PLANNED IN THE\nFLIGHT PLAN AND CONDUCTED BY THE CREW MUST BE IN THIS FORM. STUDIES, INVESTIGATIONS, OR\nEXPERIMENTS CONDUCTED AFTER THE SKYLAB MISSION WHICH USE EXISTING DATA AVAILABLE AND\nREQUIRING NO SPECIFIC MISSION SUPPORT OR PLANNING NEED NOT BE DOCUMENTED IN THIS MANNER.\nSINCE MOST INVESTIGATIONS ENVISIONED FOR EREP WILL REQUIRE SPECIFIC SENSOR ACTIVATION\nOVER SPECIFIC TEST SITES, EREP EXPERIMENTS WILL BE REQUIRED TO BE DOCUMENTED IN THE DTO\nFORMAT. CONSEQUENTLY, THIS DOCUMENT WILL INSTRUCT POTENTIAL PROPOSERS ON HOW TO\nPROPERLY DOCUMENT THEIR REQUIREMENTS SO AS TO ENSURE PROPER MISSION PLANNING, CREW\nSUPPORT, AND DATA GATHERING PLANS.\nDEFINITIONS\nPRIOR TO DISCUSSING THE INSTRUCTIONS ON HOW TO DOCUMENT PROPERLY YOUR SKYLAB EREP\nREQUIREMENTS, YOU SHOULD HAVE THE BENEFIT OF THE FOLLOWING DEFINITIONS:\nMISSION OBJECTIVES: MISSION OBJECTIVES ARE THE ENDS TOWARD WHICH EFFORTS ARE\nDIRECTED FOR EACH MISSION. MISSION OBJECTIVES ARE SPECIFIED BY THE OMSF.\nEXPERIMENTS: EXPERIMENTS ARE PLANNED INVESTIGATIONS WHICH ARE CONDUCTED INFLIGHT\nDURING MANNED SPACE MISSIONS OR WHICH ARE ESSENTIALLY CONNECTED WITH THE INFLIGHT\nSITUATION. THESE INVESTIGATIONS, WHICH ARE APPROVED BY THE MANNED SPACE FLIGHT\nEXPERIMENTS BOARD AND ASSIGNED BY THE HEADQUARTERS PROGRAM OFFICE (ML), ARE CONDUCTED TO OBTAIN RESEARCH INFORMATION WHICH CAN CONTRIBUTE TO THE ADVANCEMENT OF\nSCIENCE AND TECHNOLOGY.\n331\n\nNASA-S-71-12836-V\n\nSKYLAB/EREP DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES (CONT)\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE: THE DTO\'s ARE SCIENTIFIC, ENGINEERING, OR OPERATIONAL OBJECTIVES WHICH AMPLIFY MISSION OBJECTIVES OR DETAIL A MAJOR DEVELOPMENT PURPOSE OR\nFEATURES OF THE MISSION. THE ACCOMPLISHMENT OF A DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE WILL BE\nAN IMPORTANT CONSIDERATION IN DETERMINING THE DEGREE OF ACHIEVEMENT OF THE MISSION\nOBJECTIVE(S),\nMANDATORY DATA: MANDATORY DATA IN A DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE ARE DATA DEEMED\nESSENTIAL FOR THE EVALUATION OF THE TEST OBJECTIVE.\nHIGHLY DESIRABLE DATA: HIGHLY DESIRABLE DATA IN A DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE ARE DATA\nTHAT AID EVALUATION OF THE TEST OBJECTIVE, THESE DATA SUPPLY INFORMATION WHICH IS\nAVAILABLE FROM ALTERNATE SOURCES OR WHICH IS NOT REQUIRED FOR EVALUATION OF THE\nESSENTIAL PARIS OF THE OBJECTIVE.\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES\nTHE FOLLOWING GUIDELINES SHOULD BE USED IN DOCUMENTING AN APPROVED EXPERIMENT\nUTILIZING THE EARTH RESOURCES EXPERIMENT PACKAGE. PROPOSED EXPERIMENTS NOT YET\nAPPROVED SHOULD BE DOCUMENTED PER THE INSTRUCTIONS IN THE ERIS/EREP PROPOSAL INSTRUCTION HANDBOOK. THOSE INVESTIGATORS SHOULD BE AWARE, HOWEVER, THAT EVENTUALLY,\nAPPROVED EXPERIMENTS WILL HAVE 10 CONSIDER THE FOLLOWING GUIDELINES WHICH ARE INTENDED\n10 ENSURE THE ACQUISITION OF ALL DATA REQUIRED 10 FULFILL THE OBJECTIVE.\nTITLE: A VERY SHORT DESCRIPTION OF THE EXPERIMENT WHICH CAN BE USED 10 LIST OR DISCUSS THE EXPERIMENT WITH A MINIMUM OF WORDS, e.g., "SEVERE STORMS," "ZERO GRAVITY\nFLAMMABILITY," "WHITE LIGHT CORONAGRAPH."\n\n332\n\nNASA-71-13273-V\n\nSKYLAB/EREP DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES (CONT)\nPURPOSE: A VERY SHORT PARAGRAPH OF ONE OR TWO SENTENCES WHICH EXPLAINS THE INTENTION OF THE EXPERIMENT IN GENERAL TERMS, e.g., "10 MEASURE ELECTROCARDIOGRAPH\nPOTENTIALS IN ZERO g," "TO QUANTITATIVELY EVALUATE SPECIFIC REGIONS OF THE IR SPECTRA\nFOR APPLICATION 10 EARTH RESOURCES SENSING FROM ORBITAL ALTITUDES." ANY MORE DETAIL\nCAN BE DESCRIBED IN THE "BACKGROUND" SECTION OF THE DTO.\nFUNCTIONAL OBJECTIVES (FO\'s): THIS SECTION SHOULD CONTAIN EACH SEPARATE PART OF THE\nOVERALL OBJECTIVE. THE TOTAL OF ALL FO\'s CONSTITUTE THE ENTIRE DTO. IDEALLY, EACH\nFO IS A SCHEDULABLE ENTITY WHICH CAN SATISFY ALL OR PART OF THE OVERALL OBJECTIVE.\nBY "SCHEDULABLE" WE MEAN 11 MUST OCCUR AT A CERTAIN TIME, AT A CERTAIN PLACE, OR\nASSOCIATED WITH A SPECIFIC SET OF CONDITIONS; e.g., "FO 1, OBTAIN VISIBLE IR SPECTRA\nOF A SEVERE STORM." "FO 2, OBTAIN VISIBLE IR SPECTRA OF AN 0L SLICK." 11 IS IMPORTANT\n10 BREAK DOWN THE DTO AS CLEARLY AS POSSIBLE INTO DEFINITIVE FO\'s BECAUSE THE REMAINING SECTIONS ARE WRITTEN 10 ADDRESS SPECIFIC CONDITIONS, CRITERIA, AND DATA FOR THESE\nFO\'s.\nTEST CONDITIONS: EACH OF THE "TEST CONDITIONS" SECTIONS SHOULD LIST ALL OF THE NECESSARY CONDITIONS WHICH MUST BE ARRANGED OR OCCUR 10 ADEQUATELY SATISFY EACH FUNCTIONAL\nOBJECTIVE. THESE CONDITIONS SHOULD INCLUDE ITEMS SUCH AS THE FOLLOWING:\n- SPACECRAFT\n- TEST SITE\n- CREWS\n- GROUND TRUTH\n- TIME OF YEAR OR SEASON\n- CELESTIAL CONDITIONS\n- TRAJECTORY\nMISSION CONTROL\n- SENSOR(S)\n333\n\nNASA-71-13274-V\n\nSKYLAB/EREP DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES (CONT)\n-CLOUD COVER\ni-SNOW COVER\n-VEHICLE ATTITUDE\nBE SPECIFIC IF YOU MUST, BUT BE SURE TO INDICATE YOUR FLEXIBILITY IF, IN FACT, YOUR\nEXPERIMENT CAN BE SO.\nSUCCESS CRITERIA: THE INFORMATION YOU PUT INTO THIS SECTION WILL BE THAT USED 10\nWEIGH THE OVERALL SUCCESS OF YOUR PART OF THE MISSION OBJECTIVES. 11 IS IMPORTANT\nTHAT YOU LIST ONLY THOSE EVENTS WHICH MUST TAKE PLACE IN ORDER 10 SATISFY THE\nPURPOSE OF EACH FO. THE "SUCCESS CRITERIA" SHOULD ADDRESS THE MINIMUM CONDITIONS\nAND DATA NEEDED AS WELL AS PERTINENT EVALUATIONS AND CONCLUSIONS. IT IS POSSIBLE\n10 HAVE EVERYTHING YOU THOUGHT WAS REQUIRED BUT STILL NOT BE ABLE 10 DETERMINE\nTHE DESIRED RESULTS. IF ONLY ONE PASS OVER A SITE IS REQUIRED TO SATISFY THE FO BUT\nFIVE WERE DESIRED, INDICATE THIS IN YOUR REQUIREMENT. CARE SHOULD BE TAKEN NOT 10\nWRITE SUCCESS CRITERIA WHICH YOU KNOW OR SUSPECT CAN NEVER BE MET.\nDATA REQUIREMENTS: THIS IS POSSIBLY THE MOST IMPORTANT PORTION OF THE DTO IN THAT\nTHE MSC SUPPORTING ORGANIZATIONS MUST REVIEW AND EVALUATE EACH DTO 10 SEE HOW\nTHEY WILL SUPPORT YOUR REQUIREMENTS. 11 IS THIS SECTION WHICH WILL INDICATE LONG\nLEADTIME ITEMS SUCH AS SPECIAL PROCESSING EQUIPMENT OR TECHNIQUES WHICH MUST BE\nDEVELOPED OR SPECIAL PROCEDURES WHICH MUST BE ESTABLISHED. THIS SECTION SHOULD\nOUTLINE TYPE AND QUANTITY OF DATA NEEDED 10 SATISFY THE OBJECTIVES AND ANY SPECIAL\nPROCESSING OR HANDLING TECHNIQUES WHICH NEED 10 BE IDENTIFIED. YOU SHOULD CONSIDER\nTHE FOLLOWING:\n-PHOTO REQUIREMENTS\n-MAGNETIC TAPE\n-ASTRONAUT VOICE TAPES AND LOGS\n-TRAJECTORY SUPPORT DATA\n-VEHICLE PARAMETERS\n334\n\nNASAS-71-12834-V\n\nSKYLAB/EREP DETAILED TEST OBJECTIVES (CONT)\nGROUND TRUTH DATA\n- AIRCRAFT DATA\n- SPECIAL HANDLING REQUIREMENTS\n- SPECIAL PROCESSING REQUIREMENTS\nBACKGROUND\n11 IS IN THIS SECTION THAT YOU SHOULD INCLUDE ALL THE DETAILS WHICH SUPPORT YOUR EXPERIMENT EXPLAINING ITS SCIENTIFIC WORTH, HOW IT MIGHT FIT IN WITH OTHER INVESTIGATIONS, AND\nIN GENERAL, EXPLAIN 10 THE READER, THE LOGIC AND RATIONALE WHICH HAS GONE INTO THE\nDEVELOPMENT OF THIS OBJECTIVE. ELABORATION OF MATHEMATICAL EQUATIONS ARE DISCOURAGED\nBUT SHOW ENOUGH INFORMATION 10 JUSTIFY YOUR EXPERIMENT.\n\n335\n\nNASA-S-7 1-12808-V\n\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE EXAMPLE\nEXPERIMENT S063 UV MRGLOW HORIZON PHOTOGRAPHY\nPURPOSE\nTHE PURPOSE IS 10 PHOTOGRAPH THE EARTH OZONE LAYER AND THE TWILIGHT A I RGLOW IN\nVISIBLE AND ULTRAVIOLET (UV) LIGHT. THESE PHOTOS, MADE ON A GLOBAL SCALE, WILL BE\nVALUABLE IN THE STUD ES OF V ISI BLE AND UV MECHANISMS, AND KNOWLEDGE MAY ALSO\nBE GAINED PERTAINING 10 UPPER ATMOSPHERIC MOVEMENTS WHICH SEEM 10 BE ASSOCIATED\nWITH AIRGLOW VARIATIONS.\nTHE FUNCTIONAL OBJECTIVES ARE AS FOLLOWS:\nFO 1) PHOTOGRAPH THE EARTH\'S OZONE ATMOSPHERE AT UV\nWAVELENGTHS AND PHOTOGRAPH THE EARTH AND ITS\nATMOSPHERE AT VlSI BLE WAVELENGTHS\nF2)\n\nPHOTOGRAPH THE EARTH\'S TWILIGHT AIRGLOW AT\nVlSI BLE WAVELENGTHS\n*WEIGHTING FACTORS BASED ON 100%\n\n336\n\n(40%)*\n\n(30%)*\n\nPHOTOGRAPH THE EARTH\'S TWILIGHT AIRGLOW AT\nUV WAVELENGTHS\n\nF3)\n\n\t\n\n\t\n\n\t\n\n(30%)*\n\nNASA-S-71-12809-V\n\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE EXAMPLE (CONT)\nTEST CONDITIONS\nFO 1) EXPERIMENT ASSEMBLY 1 CONSI STING IN PART OF TWO CAMERAS, ONE FOR TAKING\nUV PHOTOGRAPHS AND THE OTHER FOR TAKING REGULAR COLOR PHOTOGRAPHS, WILL\nBE USED. THE UV CAMERA WILL BE MOUNTED AT THE ANTI-SOLAR SCIENTIFIC Al RLOCK (SAL). THE COLOR CAMERA WILL BE MOUNTED IN THE WARDROOM WINDOW OF\nTHE ORBITAL WORKSHOP (OWS).\nTEN DAYLIGHT Z-LV(E) PASSES WILL BE REQUIRED. THESE PASSES MAY BE THE SAME\nAS EARTH RESOURCES EXPERIMENTS PACKAGE (EREP) Z-LV(E) PASSES IF THE CREW\n1 S AVAILABLE.\nTRACKING WILL BE ACCOMPLISHED BY AN ASTRONAUT WHO WILL KEEP THE OPTICAL\nSIGHT ON THE UV CAMERA POINTED AT SOME FEATURE ON OR NEAR THE EARTH\'S SURFACE PER PROCEDURES CONTAINED IN THE S063 EXPERIMENT OPERATIONS HANDBOOK\n(EOH).\nTHE OPTICAL SIGHTING DEVICE WILL BE KEPT POINTED 10 WITHIN TBD DEGREE ON A\nCHOSEN TRACKING FEATURE\n\n337\n\nNASA-S-71-12810-V\n\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE EXAMPLE (CONT)\nIMAGE MOTION CONTROL (I MC) WILL BE MAINTAINED BY THE EXPERIMENTER THROUGH\nTHE DURATION OF THE EXPOSURE. REQUIRED TRACKING RATES ARE FUNCTIONS OF\nORBITAL POSITION AND TARGET ALTITUDE. APPROXIMATE AVERAGE RATES ARE\n1 DEGREE/SEC FOR THE OZONE PHOTOGRAPHY.\nTHE EARTH\'S OZONE LAYER WILL BE PHOTOGRAPHED FROM AS MANY ORBITAL POSITIONSAS POSSIBLE DURING DAYTIME.\nIT 1 S ESTIMATED THAT 15 EXPOSURES PER ORBIT CAN BE MADE. APPROXIMATELY\n10 ORBITS WILL BE REQUIRED TO COMPLETE THE 150 EXPOSURE MISSION.\nDURATIONS OF EXPOSURES WILL BE VARIED AS FILTERS AND TARGETBRIGHTNESS\nREQUI RE.\nTHE DURATION OF PERFORMANCE OF AN OZONE PHOTOGRAPHY SESSION IS ESTIMATED TO BE 30 MINUTES. THE AVERAGE TOTAL TIME FOR TAKING EACH OF THE 15\nEXPOSURES I S ESTIMATED TO BE TWO MINUTES. THIS INCLUDES ALL OPERATIONS\nSUCH AS DATA ANNOTATI ON, Fl LM ADVANCES, Fl LTER CHANGE, TARGET SELECTI ON\nAND ACQUI SITION, CAMERA ADJUSTMENT, ETC.\n\n338\n\nNASA-S-7 1-1281 1-V\n\nDETAILED TEST OBJECTIVE EXAMPLE (CONT)\nFO 2) EXPERIMENT ASSEMBLY 11 CONSI STING IN PART OF A UV CAMERA WILL BE ATTACHED\nTO THE SOLAR SAL\nAPPROXIMATELY 14 ORBITS WILL BE REQUIRED TO PERFORM THIS PORTION OF THE\nTWILIGHT AIRGLOW PHOTOGRAPHY. REQUIREMENTS FOR ADDITIONAL HARDWARE OR EXPENDITURE OF\nFUNDS MUST BE APPROVED BY THE MANAGER OF THE SKYLAB PROGRAM AND THESE TYPES\nOF REQUIREMENTS USUALLY GO THROUGH SEVERAL MANAGEMENT BOARDS FOR REVIEW AND\nEVALUATION.\nSCIENCE REQUIREMENTS PERTAINING TO MISSION PLANNING, OPERATIONS, DATA HANDLING,\nGROUND SUPPORT, AND THE LIKE ARE HANDLED IN A DIFFERENT MANNER. THE SCIENCE\nMISSIONS SUPPORT DIVISION OF S&AD WILL EVALUATE AND COORDINATE THIS TYPE OF REQUIREMENT WITH THE APPROPRIATE MSC ORGANIZATION SUCH AS THE FLIGHT CONTROL\nDIVISION, MISSION PLANNING AND ANALYSIS DIVISION, FLIGHT SUPPORT DIVISION, FLIGHT\nCREW SUPPORT DIVISION, ET CETERA. THESE VARIOUS ORGANIZATIONS HAVE SPECIFIC\nRESPONSIBILITIES FOR IMPLEMENTING CERTAIN PORTIONS OF THE OVERALL SCIENCE\nREQUIREMENTS.\nA SPECIAL PANEL HAS BEEN ESTABLISHED 10 REVIEW EREP REQUIREMENTS WITHIN THE\nSCIENCE AND APPLICATIONS DIRECTORATE AND AIR THESE WITH THE VARIOUS IMPLEMENTING ORGANIZATIONS MENTIONED ABOVE. THIS PANEL IS CALLED THE S&AD EREP REQUIREMENTS PANEL AND IS CHAIRED BY MANFRED VON EHRENFRIED, CHIEF, SCIENCE REQUIREMENTS\nAND OPERATIONS BRANCH, EXTENSION 5851.\nANOTHER SPECIAL PANEL HAS BEEN ESTABLISHED BY THE FLIGHT CONTROL DIVISION TO\nVERIFY ADEQUATE FLIGHT CONTROL UNDERSTANDING OF EXPERIMENT OPERATION AND 10\nENSURE PROPER SUPPORT OF THE DATA REQUIREMENTS. THIS GROUP IS CALLED THE\nEXPERIMENT OPERATIONS PANEL AND IS CHAIRED BY JAMES SAULTZ, CHIEF, EXPERIMENT\nSYSTEMS BRANCH, EXTENSION 4746.\n\n353\n\nNASA- S-71 - 127 64-V\n\nREQUIREMENTS IMPLEMENTATION
